<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A state of utter disorder, advanced disorganization and confusion

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:anarchisme.html>anarchisme</a> (109706)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:anarchisme.html>anarchisme</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:anarchie.html>anarchie</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anarchy</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">-isme</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">ism</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">anarchia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀναρχία</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anarkhía</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anarchy, lack of a leader</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀν-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">an-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">without</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀρχός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">arkhós</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">leader</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:anchorman.html>anchorman</a> (71197)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">anchor</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/anchorman" class="extiw" title="w:anchorman"><a href = vnd.unilang:anchorman.html>anchorman</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/anchorman" class="extiw" title="w:anchorman">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:anchorman.html>anchorman</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">anchormen</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The main host of a television or radio program, particularly one relating to the broadcast of news.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">athletics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The most reliable runner in a relay team, usually the one that <a href = vnd.unilang:runs.html>runs</a> last.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The person on a ship in charge of the anchor. <span class="defdate">[10th or 11th century]</span></li></ol>

</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(media)</span> <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:beroep.html>beroep</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vaste.html>vaste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:presentator.html>presentator</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dagelijks.html>dagelijks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:uitgezonden.html>uitgezonden</a> nieuwsrubriek/<a href = vnd.unilang:journaal.html>journaal</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:televisie.html>televisie</a>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh"><a href = vnd.unilang:andar.html>andar</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*anþeraz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">other</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">annar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sette_Comuni" class="extiw" title="w:Sette Comuni">Sette Comuni</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> other

***anderhalf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:anderhalf.html>anderhalf</a> (4628)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></i>. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>Ander</a></i>, while usually meaning <i>other</i>, also <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an archaic meaning as “second”. <i><a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>Half</a></i> means more specifically “half before”. Therefore, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:anderhalf.html>anderhalf</a></i> means literally “half before the second”, but this meaning <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> no longer generally understood in this way.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:anderhalf.html>anderhalf</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>one and a <a href = vnd.unilang:half.html>half</a></li></ol>

<a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waartegen.html>waartegen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>bot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bestand.html>bestand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>. <b><a href = vnd.unilang:pathologie.html>pathologie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>bot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aanwezig.html>aanwezig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:waardoor.html>waardoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bot.html>bot</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zo.html>zo</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:broos.html>broos</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wordt.html>wordt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:normale.html>normale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:krachten.html>krachten</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zoals.html>zoals</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wandelen.html>wandelen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> rechtstaan (<a href = vnd.unilang:bijvoorbeeld.html>bijvoorbeeld</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bij.html>bij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:osteoporose.html>osteoporose</a>, botmetastase).</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The causes of bone fractures are to be classified under two great categories. On the one side as a consequence of great external forces (for example an accident) that are exerted upon the bone and against which the bone <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unable to withstand. <b>On the other hand</b> there can be present a pathology of the bone through which the bone becomes so fragile that it <a href = vnd.unilang:breaks.html>breaks</a> under the influence of normal forces such as walking and standing up (for example due to osteoporosis, bone metastasis).</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:andijvie.html>andijvie</a> (77386)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">endivie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">endive</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">endivia</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Late_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Late Latin">Late Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">intibus</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἔντυβον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">éntubon</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Ultimately of uncertain origin, indeed perhaps <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Τῦβι</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Tûbi</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the month of Tybi, roughly January</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Egyptian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Egyptian language">Egyptian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="egy">tꜣ-ꜥꜣbt</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">the month of Tybi</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>endive, <i>Cichorium endivia</i> (salad vegetable)</li></ol>

<ul><li>Sometimes masculine in Southern Dutch.</li></ul>

***android.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>android</a> (47848)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:New Latin">New Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">androides</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνδρός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">andrós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (genitive of <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνήρ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">anḗr</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, “man”) + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">-ειδής</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-eidḗs</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εἶδος</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eîdos</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">form, image, shape, appearance, look</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Note the form <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνδρώδης</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">andrṓdēs</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">manly</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> already existed in <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span>. Synchronically, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">andro-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">-oid</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>android</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">androids</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A robot that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> designed to look and act like a human being (not necessarily male)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">droid</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>android</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en comparative-form-of" lang="en">more <a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>android</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en superlative-form-of" lang="en">most <a href = vnd.unilang:android.html>android</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Possessing human qualities.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">anatomy<span class="ib-comma">,</span> in pelvimetry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Of the pelvis, having a narrow anterior segment and a heart-shaped brim, typically found in the male.</li></ol>
</body>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:aneurysm.html>aneurysm</a> (85165)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνεύρυσμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aneúrusma</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a widening, a dilatation</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνευρύνω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aneurúnō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to dilate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἀνά</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">aná</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">εὐρύς</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">eurús</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wide</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">pathology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An abnormal blood-filled swelling of an artery or vein, resulting from a localized weakness in the wall of the vessel.</li></ol>

***angelica.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:angelica.html>angelica</a> (15721)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:angelica.html>angelica</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">angelicas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A tall plant, with hollow stems, genus <i><a href = vnd.unilang:angelica.html>Angelica</a></i>, especially the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/garden_angelica" class="extiw" title="w:garden angelica">garden <a href = vnd.unilang:angelica.html>angelica</a></a> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:angelica.html>Angelica</a> archangelica</i>).
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">archangel</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>Candied stems of the plant, used to decorate <a href = vnd.unilang:cookies.html>cookies</a>.</li>
<li>Species of <i>Aralia</i>.</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Synonym of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">angélique</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">musical instrument</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***angora.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a> (109688)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the name of the city of <i class="Latn mention" lang="tr"><a href = vnd.unilang:ankara.html>Ankara</a></i> in Turkey, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἄγκυρα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ánkura</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">anchor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">angoras</b>)
</p>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid aaa; font-size: 90%; background: f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><div class="floatnone"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/44px-Wikipedia-logo.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="44" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/66px-Wikipedia-logo.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/63/Wikipedia-logo.png/88px-Wikipedia-logo.png 2x" data-file-width="200" data-file-height="200" /></div></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English Wikipedia <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/angora" class="extiw" title="w:angora"><a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a></a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/angora" class="extiw" title="w:angora">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<ol><li>An <a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a> cat.</li>
<li>a goat of a domesticated breed that produces mohair.</li>
<li>a rabbit belonging to the <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Angora_rabbit" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Angora rabbit"><a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>Angora</a> rabbit</a> breed, one of the oldest domestic breeds of <a href = vnd.unilang:rabbits.html>rabbits</a> in the world, raised chiefly in Europe for its <a href = vnd.unilang:silky.html>silky</a> and long hair <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a subspecies of the European rabbit, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Oryctolagus_cuniculus" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Oryctolagus cuniculus">Oryctolagus cuniculus</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The hair of <a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rabbits.html>rabbits</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a> goats, used to make textiles.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The fabric made from the hair of <a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rabbits.html>rabbits</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:angora.html>angora</a> goats.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">anxt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*angust</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*angustiz</i>.

***angsthaas.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:angsthaas.html>angsthaas</a> (17902)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:angst.html>angst</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:haas.html>haas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a loan translation of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Angsthase</i>, which could be based on the <a href = vnd.unilang:hare.html>hare</a>’s flight <a href = vnd.unilang:instinct.html>instinct</a>, but <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> usually thought to be an alteration of unattested <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">*Angsthose</i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Hose</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">trousers, <a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">bangebroek</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:shit.html>shit</a> one's <a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:angsthaas.html>angsthaas</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:angsthazen.html>angsthazen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:angsthaas.html>angsthaasje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a person who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> easily scared, scaredy-cat</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***ankerplaats.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ankerplaats.html>ankerplaats</a> (95765)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ankeren.html>ankeren</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:plaats.html>plaats</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ankerplaats.html>ankerplaats</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ankerplaats.html>ankerplaatsen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ankerplaats.html>ankerplaatsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)

***anticlimax.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:anticlimax.html>anticlimax</a> (45904)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">anti-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">climax</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:anticlimax.html>anticlimax</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">anticlimaxes</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A failed or reverse climax, <i>particularly</i>:
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">narratology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An unsatisfying resolution to a narrative, usually owing to a <i><a href = vnd.unilang:deus.html>deus</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ex.html>ex</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:machina.html>machina</a></i> or similarly trivial resolution of the main conflict.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">rhetoric</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An abrupt descent (either deliberate or unintentional) from the dignity of the idea which the speaker or writer appeared to be aiming for.</li></ol></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">partial</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">bathos</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">anticlimactic</span></li></ul>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:anticlimax.html>anticlimax</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:letterkunde.html>letterkunde</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weinig.html>weinig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spannende.html>spannende</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:soms.html>soms</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:teleurstellend.html>teleurstellende</a> ontknoping <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verhaal.html>verhaal</a></li>
